# Blood

Blood is a key resource in V Rising.

The player must continuously find new victims lest they run out of blood entirely. Feeding on a blood-carrying target (victim) will refill the player's Blood Pool to its maximum capacity of 10 liters and absorb the victim's blood type (Creature, Rogue, Warrior, etc.). Later on in the game the player unlocksBlood PotionandBlood Merlot, which allows them to store blood for later consumption. Each blood type provides different passive bonuses, with higher quality blood granting stronger bonuses. The 5 tiers of Blood Pool powers are unlocked at different percentage levels. For example, Tier IV Blood Pool powers will only be unlocked by a 90%+ blood quality victim.

The Blood Pool drains slowly over time, and faster when dealing & taking damage or using particularvampire powerssuch asBlood MendorExpose Vein. Dying will immediately incur a 1 liter Blood Pool loss. Blood drainage can be virtually paused whilst sleeping in aCoffin. Blood drain is reduced by 25% on Relaxed Difficulty.Upon running out of a non-frailed Blood Pool, the player's Blood Pool will revert to 1 liter ofFrailedblood.If their frailed Blood Pool runs out, the player's health will slowly deplete to 1 health. Feeding on any source of blood will restore the player's health regeneration.

Prior to v1.0, a player's Blood Pool could not be refilled by any means without also changing blood type & quality. However, after update 1.0, it is now an option in the endgame. By feeding on a defeatedPrimal Blood Soulfrom a Tier 2Rift Incursionin theRuins of Mortium, 5 liters of the player's current Blood Pool will be instantly refilled.

### Threshold Percentages[]

Blood Quality % required to unlock each Tier

- I:1%
- II:30%
- III:60%
- IV:90%
- V:100%


### Bonus Scaling[]

For tiers I - III, at least one variable is proportional to the quality of the given blood, down to a minimum of half the max potential bonus. For example,Worker Blood'sTier 1bonus will provide at least12%but up-to24%Increased Resource yield, the value of which ranges between 1% and 100% Blood Quality:

- 1%Blood Quality =>12%Increased Resource yield
- 30%Blood Quality =>15.6%Increased Resource yield
- 50%Blood Quality =>18%Increased Resource yield
- 99%Blood Quality =>24%Increased Resource yield
- 100%Blood Quality =>~29%Increased Resource yield (includingTier Vbonus of+20%)


### Detecting Blood Types[]

Mouse over a victim to display the blood type and blood quality percentage.

Once the player has fed on theV Blood CarrierTristan the Vampire Hunter, they will unlock theBlood Hungerability. Blood Hunger places the player in a blood detection mode, displaying the blood type icon and percentage over all victims' heads, instead of needing to mouse over.

## Blood Consumables[]

The player can consume items such asRatsandTainted Heartsto restore a small amount of their blood pool, at the cost of changing their blood type to 'frailed', losing all blood type bonuses.

Once the player has fed on theV Blood CarrierVincent the Frostbringer, they will unlockPrison Cells. By using theDominateVampire Power they can imprison high-quality human victims and repeatedly extractBlood Potions/Blood Merlotsfrom them. Allowing for a consistent supply of high quality blood.

Once the player has fed onLucile the Venom Alchemist, they will additionally be able to mixBlood Potionsvia theBlood Homogenizer. This allows for fusing one of the blood traits in a potion into another. If theblood qualityof the secondary potion is 90% or higher, theIVbonus will also be infused.

## Servants[]

Servants increase in power and effectiveness with blood quality level. For more info seeServants.

## Blood Pool Examples[]

# V Rising

V RisingDeveloper / PublisherStunlock StudiosEngineUnityVersion1.1.8.0PlatformPC, Steam, PS5, GeForce NowRelease dateMay 17th 2022(Early Access)May 8th 2024(PC Full Release)June 11th 2024(PS5 Full Release)GenreSurvival, Mythology, Adventure, Action, Survival, Open World, Moddable, SandboxModeSingleplayer, Multiplayer, Online Co-Op, Local Co-OpRatingVery PositiveMediaDigitalV Risingis an open-world top-down hack'n'slash sandbox survival game developed and published byStunlock Studios. It was released inEarly Accesson Steam for Microsoft Windows on May 17, 2022.

As part of V Rising's firstHalloween Event, the game was first made free-to-play from October 28th to November 1st, 2022, and later again from September 12th to September 16th, 2024.

A year after its early access release on May 17th, 2023, it received its first major update: The Secrets ofGloomrot.

The following year it would receive another large update when it fully released on Steam onMay 8th, 2024.

V Rising launched on PS5 onJune 11th, with players who pre-ordered theCastlevania Editionor theComplete edition(allDLCs) getting a head start onJune 6th, 2024.

The latestUpdate 1.1: Invaders of Oakveilhas been the biggest to date, reworking many of the game's systems and combat stats. It released onApril 28th, 2025.

## Premise[]

| “ | Awaken after hundreds of years of slumber, weakened and thirsty for blood. Gather a clan of allies online or play the part of the lone wolf as you explore a vast open world of dark horrors and, worse: the deadly sunlight. Raise a mighty castle worthy of your name, and convert the most promising humans into thralls to serve within it.Pillage villages, raid bandit camps and traverse the territories of supernatural beasts. Drink their blood to steal their knowledge and power to become the greatest predator of them all.In a world of conflict, only one vampire shall reign supreme.Dare you challenge the throne of Dracula? | ” |

## Wiki Quick Navigation[]

## DLC[]

The game currently has 2 free and 5 paidDLC Packs. All DLC contents are only cosmetic in nature. DLC exclusive items such asArmours,Cloaks,Hats&Saddles(Horseskins) are tradeable among players on the same server.

## System Requirements[]

### Minimum[]

- Requires a 64-bit processor and operating system
- OS: Windows 10 64 bit
- Processor: Intel Core i5-6600, 3.3 GHz or AMD Ryzen 5 1500X, 3.5 GHz
- Memory: 12 GB RAM
- Graphics: NVIDIA GeForce GTX 750 Ti, 2 GB or AMD Radeon R7 360, 2 GB
- DirectX: Version 11
- Network: Broadband Internet connection
- Storage: 7 GB available space


### Recommended[]

- Requires a 64-bit processor and operating system
- OS: Windows 10 64 bit
- Processor: Intel Core i5-11600K, 3.9 GHz or AMD Ryzen 5 5600X, 3.7 GHz
- Memory: 12 GB RAM
- Graphics: NVIDIA GeForce GTX 1070, 8 GB or AMD Radeon RX 590, 8 GB
- DirectX: Version 11
- Network: Broadband Internet connection
- Storage: 7 GB available space

# Abilities

Abilitiesin V Rising come in the form ofWeaponSkills,Spells,PassivesandVampire Powers.Skills are tied to the currently equipped weapon, whereas Spells, Passives and Vampire Powers depend on knowledge acquired from slayingV Bloods. Your spells and power layout is changed via the Spellbook.

The game currently offers 14 unique weapon types, 6 spell schools, 24 passives and 12 vampire powers to choose from. Of which the player can have up to 3 Weapon Skills, 1 travel spell, 2 basic spells, 1 ultimate spell, 12 vampire powers and 5 passives equipped at once. (Although only one Vampire Power may be active at a time.) Ultimates and defensive spells cannot crit. All abilities and actions can be cancelled early (default key X).

Read the latestpatch notesfor changes inUpdate 1.1.

## Weapon Skills & Feeding[]

Equippingaweaponwill grant your vampire up to 3 weapon skills that differ based on type of weapon equipped. Not having a weapon equipped will leave you with only theUnarmedPrimary Attack ability (SeeWeapon Skillsfor more details).

You can also feed on living beings below 25% health to fill yourblood pool. Doing so turns you briefly immaterial and replaces your Primary Attack with theBiteability, which ends the feeding early and kills the target instantly.If feeding on aV Blood Carrier, you become invulnerable during the channel.

## Vampire Powers[]

### Shapeshifting Powers[]

### Blood Powers[]

## Spells & Passives[]

You start the game with the basic travel spellVeil Of Shadow, and soon thereafter unlockShadowbolt&Blood Ritefrom the Blood Magic School. No ultimate spells orPassive Slotsare unlocked through quests, you'll need to defeatV Blood Carriersto unlock them along with the rest of Spellbook's Magic Schools.Additionally, after theGloomrotupdate spells may be modified withJewelsthat can empower their effects and add new ones.

### Spell School Mastery[]

Spell School Mastery was introduced in Update 1.1. These are passive abilities you automatically obtain as you spend 3, 5, and 7 Spell Points within a Spell School in the Spellbook.Spell Points may be reset at theAltar of Recollection. Doing so resets your mastery passives.

### Passives[]

Passives are unlocked by spendingStygian Shards&Greater Stygian Shardsobtained throughRift Incursionsat theAltar of Stygian Awakening. However, they also requirePassive Slotsto use. The altar and the first slot both unlock from feeding onGeneral Elena the Hollow.

## Spellbook[]

## Soul Shards[]

Soul Shards are unique pieces ofJewelrythat drop from endgameV Blood Carriers. These magic sources are so powerful that they replace the player's ultimate ability with a new one while equipped. In Update 1.1, this replacement is now optional.

- Soul Shard of Solarus|Summon Fallen Angel
- Soul Shard of the Winged Horror|Voidquake Vortex
- Soul Shard of the Monster|Eye of the Storm
- Soul Shard of the Serpent|Serpent's Kiss
- Soul Shard of Dracula|Blood Storm

# Jewels

JewelsBloodboundYes (if equipped)TeleportableYesSalvageableYesMax Stack Size1DescriptionTier 4 Jewel

Jewelsare powerful magical artifacts that can be socketed into any non-ultimate spell to amplify and modify its effects.

They can be equipped and replaced at any time with no cost associated, which encourages the player to experiment and swap their spell jewels.

Spell jewels can only be socketed into unlocked spells, but will remain socketed after spell point resets at theAltar of Recollection.

Jewels come in 4 tiers;Tier 1,Tier 2,Tier 3, &Tier 4.Each tier corresponds to the number of modifiers it has.For example,Tier 2 Jewels will have 2 modifiers.

Modifiers themselves also come in 5 tiers, though some unique modifiers only have 1 tier. It is speculated that higher tier Jewels possess a greater chance of rolling higher tier modifiers.

They're always found in Golden Chests &Caravancontainers, and commonly drop fromV Blood Carriers, duringRift Incursionsand rarely even regularenemies. No matter how they're acquired, the jewel's name, its modifiers, and their respective tiers are always randomized.

Not to be confused withJewelry.

## Jewelcrafting & Fusion[]

Jewels can be crafted at theJewelcrafting Table, see its page for recipes.

- Tier 2 Jewelcrafting requires slayingRaziel the Shepherd(level 57).
- Greater Tier 3 Jewelcrafting requires slayingMairwyn the Elementalist(level 70).
- Primal Tier 4 Jewelcrafting requires slayingGeneral Valencia the Depraved(level 84).


They may also be fused at theFusion Forge, allowing you to move Jewel Modifiers between two Jewels for the same Spell.

## List of all Jewel Modifiers[]

Credit to Tipcat & Vinn5162 for collecting the modifier data

# Equipment

Thispage lists allEquipmentinV Rising, includingWeapons,Armours,Jewelry,Cloaks,Hats&Bags.For a list of resources, seeItems.

The main stat of any equipment is itsGear Level. It determines the overall damage output as well as damage taken from NPCenemies, but not players. Armours & Cloaks have a corresponding cosmetic slot, that allow for changing their appearance and colour.

## Legendary Artifact Weapons[]

Artifacts are uniquely named weapons withweapon skillmodifications. They are crafted at theAncestral ForgeusingLegendary Artifact shards, which have a 15% chance of dropping from Tier 2Rift Incursionsas well asEpic Ancestral Weapon Shardpurchases from theVampire Merchant.

# Items

This page lists all inventory items, reagents, consumables, etc. and their recipes. Item stacks can be split evenly with the middle mouse button, and they can be pinned in the UI. You can take all items from aStorage Containerwith the default key Q. Finally,Crafting & Refinementrecipes can be disabled at each station.SeeEquipmentfor a list of equippable items,Waygatesfor teleportable items, andVendorsfor buyable items.

# V Blood Carriers

| “ | V Blood units are a cornerstone of the V Rising experience, truly terrifying specimens of both monsters and men that stalk the lands of Vardoran.They are the apex predators of the wilderness. They are the stalwart champions who will try to stand against the vampiric tide and challenge our rule. The pillars of society, leaders, and symbols of strength that dominate the civilized world.[1] | ” |
| - | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | - |

This page lists allV Blood Carriers. for a list of all non-V BloodEnemies, see its respective page.Tracking V Bloods is done through the V Blood Menu (default key K) after completing theJournalquestGetting Ready for the Hunt. At 50% health, V Bloods spawn at least 3Blood Orbs, restoring 7.5% max health on pick-up.

OnRelaxed Difficultythey deal 40% less damage & have 20% less health. OnBrutal Difficultythey deal 70% more damage, have 25% more health, are 3 levels higher and often have more abilities and combat behaviours.

# Vendors

Vendors(also known as dealers, merchants or traders) can be found acrossVardoranselling a wide variety ofItemsin exchange for specific currencies. You need to be inHuman FormorGrandma Formto interact with some vendors. In earlier versions ofV Rising, damage fromSilver Sicknesswould break the disguise, making it difficult to trade. This is no longer the case.

ExcludingTreasure HunterandVampire Merchants, there are four main types of vendors in each region (Farbane Woods,Dunley Farmlands,Silverlight Hills):

- Book Vendor: Sells Recipes to unlock at aResearch Desk,StudyorAthenaeum.
- Herbs & Potions Vendor: SellsSeeds,Brews&Potions.
- Gem Vendor: SellsCrude,RegularorFlawless Gems.
- Goods Vendor: SellsFish, various rare resources and exclusiveHats.


Treasure Hunteris a special vendor inGloomrot Northwho sells Sanguine Weapon blueprints, unique tier 3Cloaks, and high end main vendor items.Vampire Merchantsare special vendors inRuins of Mortiumwho sellRare Weapon ShardsandEpic Weapon Shards.

Vendors sell fixed quantities of items, varying by category. They will refresh their stock of items every 55 mins. For some categories, all variations are always purchaseable, while for others, only a partial selection are offered, chosen randomly each refresh. (for example: if the vendor sells three different weapons, he will refresh his stock with a new random selection of three weapons).

All vendors only accept one currency at their store. The currency used by the main vendors depends on the location of their store:

- Farbane Woods VendorsacceptCopper Coins
- Dunley Farmlands VendorsacceptSilver Coins
- Silverlight Hills VendorsacceptGoldsun Coins
- Treasure Hunter VendoracceptsGoldsun Coins
- Vampire Merchant (Rare)accepts750Stygian Shardsfor each shard.
- Vampire Merchant (Epic)accepts1500Greater Stygian Shardsfor each shard.


## Trivia[]

- Vendors (Early Access)

# Servants

Servants are created using aServant Coffin. Servants can be given commands and tasks to acquire resources for the castle. In order to give commands to your servants you must build aCastle Throne.

The maximum number of servants depends on the level of theCastle Heart. Be careful to use servant lock doors on the exterior of your castle/territory. Servants will freely open and close any doors that are not of the servant lock door type. LikeHorses, Servants can be given custom names.

Servants will be moved alongside the castle when using theCastle Relocation Heart.

## How to Capture a Servant[]

Dominateis aVampire Powerthat allows you to subdue lifeforms with an activeblood typeand convert them into loyalServantsorPrisoners. However, only human andsomedraculin targets may become Servants.

To successfully subdue a target for conversion to aServant, you must first reduce their health below 30%, activateDominate, and channel theDominate Spell(default key R) to dominate the target. The target may still attack during the channel.

Once a target is subdued they will enter a neutral, dormant state where their attacks are disabled, but they can still take damage fromenemies. They're then able to be placed in aServant Coffinorimprisoned.

Waygatesare unavailable while a target is subdued, it is therefore recommended to use theDusk Callerconsumableto transport the target to an emptyPrison Cellalmost immediately, or useCave Passages.

Once placed in a coffin the conversion process will begin, taking 20 (10) minutes in real time. (Crypt Flooring)It costs100 (50)Blood Essenceto convert (revive) a Servant. Servants cannot be revived while the"Castle Under Attack"status effectis active.

## Expertise Range Table[]

A Servant's expertise is determined randomly on conversion, based on theirblood quality.

Expertise will influence 4 things:Max Health,Physical Power,Hunt Proficiency&Loot. The health and power values are increased by the percentage directly. Whereas the Hunt Proficiency increase is a flat amount. For example, a Gear Level 20 Servant with 10% expertise, will have a total of 210 Hunt Proficiency.Finally, expertise also increases the amount of loot gained from successful hunts by half the % value.

| Blood Quality | Expertise |
| ------------- | --------- |
| 100%          | 37% - 44% |
| >99.5%        | 36% - 44% |
| 98%           | 36% - 43% |
| 97%           | 35% - 43% |
| 96%           | 34% - 42% |
| 95%           | 34% - 42% |
| 94%           | 34% - 41% |
| 93%           | 33% - 40% |
| 92%           | 32% - 39% |
| 91%           | 31% - 38% |
| 90%           | 30% - 37% |
| 86-89%        | 29% - 35% |
| 81-85%        | 26% - 32% |

| Blood Quality | Expertise |
| ------------- | --------- |
| 76-80%        | 24% - 31% |
| 71-75%        | 22% - 26% |
| 65%-70%       | 20% - 24% |
| 60-64%        | 18% - 23% |
| 55-59%        | 16% - 19% |
| 49% - 54%     | 14% - 17% |
| 45%- 48%      | 12% - 15% |
| 40-44%        | 12% - 14% |
| 31-39%        | 10% - 13% |
| 21-30%        | 8% - 10%  |
| 11-20%        | 7% - 9%   |
| 1-10%         | 6% - 8%   |

*The Blood Quality of an enemy as it appears in the world is always rounded down. However, on conversion it will round to the nearest integer. For example, both 90.1% and a 90.9% blood quality units will appear as 90% in the world. But once converted, the latter will round up to 91%. Unconfirmed if this allows units to round up to 100% or not.

## Servant Hunts[]

After converting a target into a servant at aServant Coffin, you can sit on aCastle Throneto send servants on hunts to locations you've visited. Servants have 100 base hunt proficiency.

You can interact with a servant to provide them gear. This increases their hunt profiency by 10 times their gear level, as well as their combat stats for castle defense. Gear Level works the same for Servants as it does for players, generally speaking, by proportionally increasing their max health and damage (physical power). SeeGear Levelfor more info.

Theonlyequipment stat that matters to servants is Gear Level. All other secondary equipment stats have no effect, including set bonuses and durability level. They have the same equipment slots available as the player except for cape and headgear. After returning from a hunt, servants will carry the loot in their inventory.

### Hunt Duration[]

The duration of a hunt affects rewards as well as the chance of success. Shorter hunts earn more resources-per-hour, but have a higher risk of failure. If a hunt is unsuccesful, the servant will likely be killed. Servants can be resurrected at their coffin for50Blood Essenceover 10 minutes.

| Hunt Duration | Loot Amount | Success Chance |
| ------------- | ----------- | -------------- |
| 2 hours       | 50%         | 0%             |
| 4 hours       | 75%         | +5%            |
| 6.5 hours     | 100%        | +10%           |
| 10 hours      | 125%        | +15%           |
| 16 hours      | 150%        | +20%           |

The completion time for a hunt is based on real-world time. It is not necessary to leave the game running, and it doesn't matter whether you play a solo "offline" game or you're on a dedicated "online" server. For example, if you start a 16-hour hunt in a solo game at 6:00 pm and immediately exit the game (stopping the solo-game "server"), the hunt will complete at 10:00 am the next day, whether or not you're playing at that time.

Prior to Update 1.1, Servants could be injured during hunts.This has now been removed from the game.

### Hunt Mission Table[]

## Blood Type & Faction Perks[]

Servants have 2 perks that each will provide a benefit when going on hunts in which the perks are active.

The first perk is based onBlood Type, and will reduce the difficulty of a Hunt in a given location by 100.The second perk is determined by their faction, ie.locationof origin, increasing loot gained from successful hunts in that region by 20%.

Blood Type Perks do not stack, so sending a diverse group of servants on hunts is advised. The supported perks of each area can be found via theCastle Throneinterface.

| Blood Type         | Servant Perk       | Description                                                                                                                                                                |
| ------------------ | ------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Worker             | Humble Appearance  | Reduces Difficulty by100when infiltrating settlements.                                                                                                                     |
| Scholar            | Sacred Resistance  | Reduces Difficulty by100when hunting in areas protected by the elements.                                                                                                   |
| Brute              | Tenacious Strength | Reduces Difficulty by100when hunting in harsh environments.                                                                                                                |
| Rogue              | Tracking Expertise | Reduces Difficulty by100when hunting in areas inhabited by creatures and demons.                                                                                           |
| Warrior / Draculin | Military Tactics   | Reduces Difficulty by100when hunting in fortified areas.                                                                                                                   |
| Corrupted          | Enemy Dependent    | Corrupted human enemies have mixed blood. Their original blood type will determine their first perk. (eg. a Corrupted Peon with Worker Blood will have Humble Appearance.) |

| Location / Faction | Servant Perk            | Description                                                                            |
| ------------------ | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Farbane Woods      | Farbane Hunter          | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Farbane Woods by20%.     |
| Dunley Farmlands   | Dunley Farmlands Hunter | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Dunley Farmlands by20%.  |
| Cursed Forest      | Cursed Forest Hunter    | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Cursed Forest by20%.     |
| Silverlight Hills  | Silverlight Hunter      | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Silverlight Hills by20%. |
| Gloomrot           | Gloomrot Hunter         | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Gloomrot by20%.          |
| Ruins of Mortium   | Ruins of Mortium Hunter | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Ruins of Mortium by20%.  |
| Oakveil Woodlands  | Oakveil Hunter          | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Oakveil Woodlands by20%. |

## Tips & Trivia[]

- Servants and the hunts they're sent on are tied to the territory'sCastle Heart. This means you can send servants from different territories to hunt at the same location simultaneously.
- Cursed Forest Hunter Perk is currently exclusive to Werewolf Workers fromGracefall Village, including those few wandering the roads ofDunley Farmlands.As a Servant they will no longer transform, only whenimprisoned.
- Corrupted humanenemieswith theOakveil Hunter Perk have mixed blood. Their original blood type will determine their first perk.
- Theonlydraculin units that may be converted into Servants are Vampire Cultists, Night Maidens, Dark Temptresses and Exsanguinators.

# Journal

InV Rising, there areQueststo help guide the player into unlocking new recipes and structures. The current active Quest can be located at the Top Left corner of the HUD. The quests can be completed in any order and the rewards for that quest will be presented immediantly upon completing them, but otherwise only one quest at a time will be shown. Quest unlocks can be granted via theServer SettingUnlockedAchievements

# Rift Incursions

| “ | Use your map to track Rift Incursions within the Ruins of Mortium. The Legion of Nocturn channels Dracula's power to summon powerful entities from the Shadow Realm. Destroy these Rifts to obtain ancestral weapons and stygian shards. | ” |
| - | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | - |

Rift Incursionsare portals to theShadow Realmopened through dark rituals involving blood crystals. In these world events you will face off againstDracula'sLegion of Noctum- hordes of draculin vampires & monsters. 2 smaller blood crystals will be connected to the main blood crystal in the centre, indicating their location.Destroy them by defeating enemies to end the ritual.

At the end of an incursion, a (brutal difficulty) imitation of a V Blood Carrier will be summoned, known as Lesser and Primal Blood Souls. (Tier 1  and Tier 2 respectively)Defeating and feeding on the blood soul will destroy the blood crystal and end the Rift Incursion.

Rift Incursions come in 2 tiers. The game recommends you must be at least level 57 for Tier 1, and 83 for Tier 2 incursions. With more elite Draculin being summoned in Tier 2.TheEye of Mortiumallows the player to track when Rift Incursion events will be active inRuins of Mortium.

## Rewards[]

Tier 1:

- Stygian Shards(amount varies with the # of players present as well asServer Settings.)
- High chance ofTier 2 Jewels, low chance ofTier 3 Jewels
- 20% chance to get a randomStudyBlueprint.
- 66.6% chance to get aRare Weapon Shard.


Tier 2:

- Greater Stygian Shards(amount varies with the # of players present as well asServer Settings.)
- High chance ofTier 2 Jewels, medium chance ofTier 3 Jewels, very low chance ofTier 4 Jewels.
- 21% chance to get a randomAthenaeumBlueprint.
- 66.6% chance to get aRare Weapon Shard, 18.4% to get aEpic Weapon Shard& 15% chance to get aLegendary Artifact Shard.
- +5 liters refill of currentBlood Pooland +750Soul Sharddurability upon feeding on the Primal Blood Soul.


## Blood Souls[]

### Lesser Blood Souls[]

Errol the Stonebreaker,Rufus the Foreman,Keely the Frost Archer,Goreswine the Ravager,Lidia the Chaos Archer,Polora the Feywalker,Quincey the Bandit King,Vincent the Frostbringer,Tristan the Vampire Hunter,Kriig the Undead General

### Primal Blood Souls[]

Leandra the Shadow Priestess,Bane the Shadowblade,Frostmaw the Mountain Terror,Jade the Vampire Hunter,Octavian the Militia Captain,Domina the Blade Dancer,Angram the Purifier,Foulrot the Soultaker,Ungora the Spider Queen,Ben the Old Wanderer,Willfred the Werewolf Chief,Terrorclaw the Ogre

# Prison Cell

Prison CellRoomPrisonResources8Iron Ingot2Reinforced PlankUnlocked ByVincent the Frostbringer

## How to capture a Prisoner[]

TheVampire PowerDominateallows you to Subdue lifeforms with an activeblood typetargets and convert them into loyalServantsorPrisoners.

To successfully Subdue a target for conversion to aServant, you must first reduce their health below 30%, activateDominate, and channel theDominate Spell(default key R) to dominate the target. The target may still attack during the channel.

Once a target is dominated / Subdued they will enter a neutral, dormant state where their attacks are disabled, ready forimprisonment. While subdued they can still take damage, so it is recommended to useDusk Callerto transport them safely. Subdued enemies can be placed intoanyprison cell, allowing for prisoner trading between players.

Prisoners cannot be dominated or killed duringraids.

## Perks[]

- Has Matching Floor(Prison Flooring):-25%Blood Drain & Essence Extraction health costs.


## Usage[]

Once a victim has been imprisoned, multiple actions may be performed on them: Drain Blood, Extract Blood Essence, Feed Prisoner, Subdue & Kill.

### Drain Blood[]

The first, and primary use case for the Prison Cell, is to drain a victim's blood to fillEmpty Glass Bottles,creatingBlood PotionsorBlood Merlotsthe player can drink to maintain a blood type & quality equal to the victim's. This can be repeated indefinitely at the cost of-30% ~ -60%or-25% ~ -50%of theirhealth, and a+10% ~ +20%or+5% ~ +15%increase to theirmiserypercentage.

If the victim suffers too much damage and runs out of health, they will be permanently killed. It is therefore recommended to always ensure that a prisoner is well-fed before their blood is drained. Additionally, a prisoner's misery also has to be taken into account, as their damage taken will be increased by that percentage.

Assuming a full health prisoner, making aBlood Potion/Blood Merlotcan be done safely at any misery level below66%/100%, or122%/166%with thePrison Flooringbonus active. See the formula below:

MaxBloodDrainDamage%=50×(1+Misery%)×(1−FloorBonus%){\displaystyle Max\ Blood\ Drain\ Damage\ \%=50\times (1+Misery\%)\times (1-Floor\ Bonus\%)}

### Extract Blood Essence[]

The second, less relevant use case for prisoners, is to extractBlood Essencesfrom them, at a cost of-10% ~ -30%of their health and a+2% ~ +6%increase to their misery percentage.

### Feed Prisoner[]

Feeding prisoners is how their health is restored, as well as how their misery may be reduced. See below.

| Item                                                  | Health Increase                                                                                                       | Misery Reduction |
| ----------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------- |
| Rat                                                   | 20% — 30%                                                                                                             |                  |
| Fat Goby                                              | 100%                                                                                                                  |                  |
| Rainbow Trout                                         |                                                                                                                       | 10% — 15%        |
| Fierce Stinger                                        | 20% — 30%                                                                                                             | 5% — 10%         |
| Twilight Snapper                                      | 20% — 30%                                                                                                             | 10% — 15%        |
| Sage Fish                                             | 30% — 70%                                                                                                             | 10% — 20%        |
| Blood Snapper                                         | 50% — 75%                                                                                                             | 5% — 10%         |
| Swamp Dweller                                         | 10% — 100%                                                                                                            | 20% — 40%        |
| Golden River Bass                                     | 80% — 100%                                                                                                            | 15% — 25%        |
| Corrupted Fish                                        | -100% — 100%                                                                                                          | -25% — 25%       |
| Alters the blood quality of the prisoner by -2% — 2%. |                                                                                                                       |                  |
| Irradiant Gruel                                       | Increases the blood quality of a prisoner by 1% — 2%, but has a 35% chance to turn the prisoner into a raging mutant. |                  |

Perhaps counter-intuitively, if the Prisoner is fed a sufficiently high number of Corrupted Fish, (and is at 0% misery each time) it is guaranteed toeventuallyreach 100% Blood Quality. The probability of succes in n fish attempts can be calculated with a simple symmetric random walk formula:

Psuccess=1−N!(N/2)!(N/2)!⋅12N{\displaystyle P_{success}=1-{\frac {N!}{(N/2)!(N/2)!}}\cdot {\frac {1}{2^{N}}}}

### Subdue & Kill[]

Subdueing a prisoner allows them to be moved to a different Prison Cell or put in aServant Coffin.Note that conversion to aServantis irreversible. There is no option to set a prisoner free.  Finally, they may also be killed outright.

### Werewolves[]

An imprisoned human with werewolf capability will turn back into a werewolf at night. Previously this would cause them to escape their cell, but with the Oakveil expansion they now remain imprisoned, and retain their blood quality. This is enables you to drain bothWorker BloodandCreature Bloodfrom the same prisoner.

Workers fromGracefall Villagehave an increased probability of being high blood quality.

### Limitations[]

Hand of Dracula, Sanguinary Guard, Dreadhorns, Gargoyles & Worm Terror cannot beDominatedand turned into Prisoners, even though they have an activeblood type.

# Horse

HorseBloodboundNoTeleportableYesLoot LocationsArmy OutpostDawnbreak VillageCotton FarmMosswick VillageHorse TrackDunley Lumber MillBastion of DunleyMilitia CampDescriptionYou can mount horses, you can name horses, you can feed horses and be friends with them.

| “ | Keep your horse alive by supplying it with plant fibre. | ” |
| - | ------------------------------------------------------- | - |

Horses can be ridden by players. It is a much faster method of transportation than walking orWolf Form. While riding, you can useCaves.

Non-dominatedHorses require sustenance in the form of Plant Fibre to survive. To feed a horse, open the inventory menu while near a horse to  open its UI.
There you'll find 3 slots that can be filled with Plant Fibre, the amount depending on your server's stack capacity. Additionally, Horses may be renamed by clicking a button top right of the interface.

Highergear levelNPCs and player damage will knock the player off their horse. They can also be killed by them. If a horse perishes it may only be revived for a few minutes following a short channel.

If you've subdued a horse using theDominate MountVampire Power, you canRevive & Recallit at any time.

## Stats[]

Each Horse spawns with 200 Health and has 3 Stats whose values are randomized. The stats may be improved at theStables. Equipping aVampire Horse Saddlewill increase Max Speed & Acceleration stats further by 1. Default player speed is 4.0 for comparison.

| Stat           | Description                                      | min. Value | max. Value |
| -------------- | ------------------------------------------------ | ---------- | ---------- |
| Max Speed      | determines the highest speed the horse can reach | 7          | 9          |
| Acceleration   | determines how fast it reaches Max Speed         | 3.5        | 6          |
| Rotation Speed | determines how well the horse can turn           | 10.0       | 13.0       |

# Attributes

Attributesalso known asStats, determine the player's overall power in various aspects, both offensively, defensively and mobility wise. Some attributes have minimum base values, such asCorestats, but most start at 0. There are many ways to increase stats passively and actively, up to a cap.

An attributecannotsurpass its cap from passive / permanent sources. However, there are two ways of increasing an attribute's cap;Spell School MasteriesandBlood Efficiency. The latter of which is obtained from theVBonus by drinking100% Quality Bloodand/or theSanguine Mastery Passive. On the attributes screen, how close you are to reaching a stat cap is indicated by a red bar underneath the attribute. Any passive attributes beyond the cap are wasted and highlighted in red.

An attributecansurpass its cap from active / temporary sources, such asSpells. These will always have a duration or condition attached to them.

Attributes are entirely unaffected byGear Level's damage modification. See its dedicated page for more info.

## Core[]

### Max Health[]

"Your maximum amount of health."

### Physical Power[]

"Increases damage done by your physical attacks."

### Spell Power[]

"Increases damage done by your spells."

### Movement Speed[]

"Your speed when traversing the world."

### Resource Harvest Power[]

"Increases damage dealt to resources."

## Resistances[]

### Sun[]

"Increases the time you can endure the sun byX%."

- See the dedicatedSun Exposurepage for more details.


### Garlic[]

"Reduces garlic application rate when exposed to garlic byX%, while also increasing the recovery rate byX%.Additionally reduces the maximum number of garlic applications to100."

- See the dedicatedGarlic Exposurepage for more details.


### Fire[]

"Reduces damage taken from fire based attacks byX%and grant you aX%chance to nullify damage fromBurneffects."

- See the dedicatedBurnpage for more details.


### Holy[]

"Reduces damage taken from holy attacks byX%and negates up toXdamage from Holy Radiation."

- See the dedicatedHoly Radiationpage for more details.


### Silver[]

"Reduces damage taken from silver attacks byX%and allows you to withstand up toXapplications of Silver Exposure."

- See the dedicatedSilver Exposurepage for more details.


## Offensive[]

### Bonus Physical Power[]

"Increases total physical power."

### Attack Speed[]

"Increases the attack speed of primary attacks."

### Physical Critical Chance[]

"The chance to inflict a Critical Strike using weapon attacks."

### Physical Critical Power[]

"Damage modifier when inflicting a Critical Strike using weapon attacks."

### Weapon Skill Power[]

"Increases the damage done by Weapon Skills."

### Weapon Charge Gain[]

"The number of weapon charges gained when using aweapon skill.Weapon charges allows you to use a weapon skill without triggering a cooldown when stacked up to100charges."

Note: Weapon charges can be stacked above100. When free casts are triggered, you expend100charges and then gains charges for the cast.

For example, with 15 Weapon Charge Gain, casting a skill at 90 charges fully stacks it up to 105. Your next free weapon skill cast expends 100 charges, and gains you another 15. You now have 20 remaining weapon charges.

## Spell[]

### Bonus Spell Power[]

"Increases total spell power."

### Spell Critical Chance[]

"The chance to inflict a Critical Strike using spells."

### Spell Critical Power[]

"Damage modifier when inflicting a Critical Strike using spells."

### Ultimate Power[]

"Increases the effect of Ultimate spells, increasing damage, healing, shield effects and minion damage."

### Minion Damage[]

"Increases the damage output of all your summons & minions."

Skeleton Warrior/Skeleton Magehas health equal to200%of your Spell Power, and deals30%/50%of your Spell Power as magic damage. Theycannotcrit.

### Spell Charge Gain[]

"The number of spell charges gained when using a spell.Spell charges allows you to cast a spell without triggering a cooldown when stacked up to100charges."

Note: Spell charges can be stacked above100. When free casts are triggered, you expend100charges and then gains charges for the cast. Travel spells, also known asVeils, don't gain or consume charges.

For example, with 15 Spell Charge Gain, casting a spell at 90 charges fully stacks it up to 105. Your next free spell cast expends 100 charges, and gains you another 15. You now have 20 remaining spell charges.

## Speed[]

### Bonus Movement Speed[]

"Increases total movement speed."

### Shapeshift Speed[]

"Increases movement speed while shapeshifted."

### Mount Speed[]

"Increases movement speed while mounted."

## Defense[]

### Damage Reduction[]

"Reduces damage taken from all sources."

### Shield Efficiency[]

"Amplifies the effect of all shields applied on you."

## Health & Healing[]

The healing effects fromVermin Salve,Blood Rose BrewandBlood Rose Potionstack on top of each other. However, while in combat you're only able to recover up to 25% Max HP at a time. For example, if at 50% health, you can only heal up to 75% max health until you leave combat.Blood Orbsbypass this limitation.

### Bonus Maximum Health[]

"Increases total health."

### Health Regeneration[]

"The rate at which your health regenerates outside of combat."

### Healing Received[]

"Increases all healing received."

### Primary Attack Leech[]

"Health recovered when dealing damage using primary weapon attacks."

### Weapon Skill Leech[]

"Health recovered when dealing damage using weapon skills."

### Spell Leech[]

"Health recovered when dealing damage using spells."

## Utility[]

### Blood Efficiency[]

"Amplifies the effects of your activeBlood Typeand increases the maximum cap of blood effects with an equal amount."

### Blood Drain Reduction[]

"Reduces the rate at which you lose blood over time."

### Resource Yield[]

"The amount of materials obtained when harvesting resources."

## Cooldown[]

Cooldown Rateis similar to traditional cooldown reduction seen in other games, but functions differently. It speeds up how fast the cooldown timer itself ticks down, effectively making each second shorter. See the formula below:

Cooldown=BaseCooldown1+CooldownRate%{\displaystyle Cooldown={\frac {Base\ Cooldown}{1+Cooldown\ Rate\ \%}}}ExampleWith30%CooldownRate:Cooldown=10s1+0.30=7.69s{\displaystyle \ \ \ \ \ Example\ With\ 30\%\ Cooldown\ Rate:\ \ \ Cooldown={\frac {10s}{1+0.30}}=7.69s}

### Weapon Cooldown Rate[]

"Increases the rate at which Weapon Skill Cooldown recovers."

### Spell Cooldown Rate[]

"Increases the rate at which Spell Cooldown recovers."

### Veil Cooldown Rate[]

"Increases the rate at which Veil Cooldown recovers."

### Ultimate Cooldown Rate[]

"Increases the rate at which Ultimate Cooldown recovers."

# Blood Homogenizer

Blood HomogenizerResources1Primal Blood Essence8Dark Silver Ingot8Glass32Venom SapUnlocked ByLucile the Venom AlchemistDescriptionA workstation used for mixing blood.

## Overview[]

TheBlood Homogenizerprovides two slots in which you can placeBlood PotionsorBlood Merlots. You can then select one of the traits from the secondary potion to transfer onto the first potion. If theblood qualityof the secondary potion is 90% or higher, theIVbonus will also be infused. There is no additional cost for mixing potions, but the secondary potion will be consumed in the process.

## Perks[]

- In Confined Castle Room: +25% speed.

### Threshold Percentages[]

Blood Quality % required to unlock each Tier

- I:1%
- II:30%
- III:60%
- IV:90%
- V:100%


### Bonus Scaling[]

For tiers I - III, at least one variable is proportional to the quality of the given blood, down to a minimum of half the max potential bonus. For example,Worker Blood'sTier 1bonus will provide at least12%but up-to24%Increased Resource yield, the value of which ranges between 1% and 100% Blood Quality:

- 1%Blood Quality =>12%Increased Resource yield
- 30%Blood Quality =>15.6%Increased Resource yield
- 50%Blood Quality =>18%Increased Resource yield
- 99%Blood Quality =>24%Increased Resource yield
- 100%Blood Quality =>~29%Increased Resource yield (includingTier Vbonus of+20%)


---

# Stats

Statsfound in theattributestab in-game are a measure of a player's power level. They belong to the main categories "resistances", "offensive" and "defensive".

soft caps, hard caps, exceptions...

Ultimates and defensive spells cannot crit.

## Base Stats[]

- Max Health: 125
- Max Recoverable Health: 25%
- Movement speed: 4
- Resistances: 0
- Physical & Spell Power: 10
- Physical & Spell Crit chance: 5%
- crit damage increase: 50%

# Soul Shard of Dracula

Soul Shard of DraculaCategorySoul ShardGear Level25Attributes+34Spell Power+16%Blood Type Efficiency+20%Damage to Vampires15%chance on primary hit to gainBloodthirst. Can only trigger once every10s.Replaces your Ultimate Ability withBlood Storm.Durability2500BloodboundYesSalvageableNoSoul Shard of Draculais one of fiveSoul Shards, one of the most coveted and powerfulJewelryitems in V Rising.

OnOfficial ServersSoul Shards are unique, meaning only one of each type may exist at a time. This soul shard is obtained by being the first to slayDracula the Immortal King. If theserver settingis set to plentiful, it always drops.

## Soul Shard Mechanics[]

Upon equipping the jewelry, the player's ultimate ability is replaced withBlood Storm:"Become invulnerable and channel a Blood Storm for3s, launching up to25homing blood bolts at nearby enemies. Each bolt deals100%magic damage and inflictsLeech. End with a powerful nova, dealing300%magic damage and pushing enemies away."

In Update 1.1. players may replace the Soul Shard's ultimate ability freely.

The damage bonus to vampires applies to both players andenemies.

Bloodthirstincreases movement speed, damage output, attack speed, and life leech by 15% for 6 seconds.

Soul Shards lose durability over time and can only be repaired by feeding onPrimal Blood Soulsduring Tier 2Rift Incursions. Each Primal Blood Soul consumed restores 750 durability, distributed between all shards in the player's inventory. If a Soul Shard is destroyed it returns to itsV Blood Carrier, in this caseDracula.After Update 1.1 its durability loss may now be sped up or disabled via theServer Settings.

They may beteleportedoutside of raid windows, and carried while inBat Form.(toggleable in settings)

On PvP servers Soul Shards are dropped on death, and can be stolen by other players. To prevent this, they may be stored in their respective pedestals;Pedestal of Dracula.

Soul Shards are automatically destroyed if not picked up from the ground within 60 minutes.

---

# Tailor's Flooring

Tailor's FlooringMyrtleBurgundyCobaltRoomTailorResources4Plank2ClothUnlocked ByStudy

Tailor Flooringis a type ofCastle Flooravailable in V Rising. Upon changingall the flooringof a castle room, it activates theTailorRoom bonuses for related crafting and refinement structures:

- Tailoring Bench
- Leatherworking Station
- Tannery
- Advanced Tannery
- Loom
- Advanced Loom


The blueprint can be discovered / researched at theStudy, and is sold by theRural Book Merchantfor64Silver Coins.

# Castle Flooring

Castle FlooringDiamondSquareDiagonalEboniteBrick StablesWooden StablesRoyal *DLCPlague Sanctum *DLCAncient Symphony *DLCNocturnal Opulence *DLCRoomCastleResources2Stone BrickUnlocked ByExpanding my Domain(Quest)

Castle Flooringis a basic defaultCastle Flooravailable in V Rising. It is required to fill a room with flooring for it to count as a confined castle room (as well as provide a roof), though it does not matter which type of Castle floor is used, unless you are attempting to build specific rooms for their bonuses to crafting and refinement.

If placed on a a higher floor, sides which aren't connected to other floor tiles or walls will generate a balcony railing.

It is available in 10 different patterns, of which the Royal Pattern is exclusive to theDracula's Relics PackDLC, Plague Sanctum Tiles are exclusive to theSinister Evolution PackDLC, the Ancient Symphony Pattern is exclusive to theLegacy of Castlevania Premium PackDLC, and the Nocturnal Opulence Tiles are exclusive to theEternal Dominance PackDLC.

# Emery

EmeryCategoryMaterialBloodboundNoTeleportableNoSalvageableNoMax Stack Size500DescriptionEmery that can be refined intoEmber Glassat anAdvanced Furnace.

Emeryis a resource in V Rising.

## Overview[]

Emery is collected by miningEmery NodesinOakveil Woodlands. It can also drop as loot there. It is notably abundant at the west side ofVenom Blades Bastion, belowDantos the Forgebinder'sForge.

Emery requires aGear Level23 (Dark Silver) weapon tier or higher to mine. If struck too quickly, the nodes will explode, dropping damaging clusters in a wide area.  This does not affect the total amount of Emery harvested from each node, however.

Emery Golemscan be found disguised as unusually-shaped Emery deposits, turning hostile when attacked, and dropping Emery when destroyed.

## Recipes[]

| Resulting Item | Recipe                     | Crafting Source  |
| -------------- | -------------------------- | ---------------- |
| Ember Glass    | 8 (6)Venom Sap20 (15)Emery | Advanced Furnace |

## Building[]

| Structure             | Recipe                                                 |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------ |
| Redistribution Engine | 6Charged Battery80Emery                                |
| Athenaeum             | 20Schematic100Emery8Reinforced Plank4Dark Silver Ingot |

## Drops From

- Alchemist
- Dartflinger
- Dreadcleaver
- Emery Golem
- Sentinel
- Striker
- Viper

# Legendary Ancestral Weapon Shards

Legendary Ancestral Weapon ShardsThe GravecallerThe Red TwinsHand of WinterThe Thousand StormsCloud DancersWings of the FallenApocalypseThe Morning StarThe Fate DancersThe WraithbladesThe EndbringersOaksongBloodboundYesTeleportableYesSalvageable2Radium Alloy2Gold Jewelry1Spectral DustMax Stack Size1DescriptionSHATTEREDThe shards of a magical weapon. Unusable in its current state, bring to anAncestral Forgeto restore it.

## Overview[]

Legendary Ancestral Weapon Shardsare shattered weapons that can be restored into usable weapons at theAncestral Forgeor fused with other ancestrals at theFusion Forge. While they are considered to be tier eight alongside sanguine weapons (Gear Level26), they are more powerful (Gear Level30 & 33.7 Physical Power).

Legendary Ancestral Weapon Shards have a small chance (15%) to replace aEpic Ancestral Weapon Sharddrop or purchase from theVampire Merchantin northernRuins of Mortium.

As weapons that left a mark in the history ofVardoran, unlikeEpic Ancestral Weapon Shards, they have ability modifications both the second (Q) and third (E)weapon skill. They also all have a unique appearance, making them visually distinct from Sanguine or Epic Ancestral weapons.

In 1.0 they used to have fixed attributes, but in Update 1.1 they can now be swapped using the newFusion Forge.

## Possible Attribute Rolls[]

Legendary Ancestral weapons have3random attributes respectively. Each attribute has a minimum base value, which is then randomly multiplied by 1 - 5. There are 14 different attributes in total. Refer to the table below:

| Attribute           | 1     | 2     | 3     | 4      | 5    |
| ------------------- | ----- | ----- | ----- | ------ | ---- |
| Attack Speed        | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Crit Strike Chance  | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Crit Strike Power   | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Spell Crit Chance   | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Spell Crit Power    | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Max HP              | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Movement Speed      | +1.6% | +3.2% | +4.8% | +6.4%  | +8%  |
| Physical Power      | +2%   | +4%   | +6%   | +8%    | +10% |
| Spell Cooldown Rate | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Spell Leech         | +2%   | +4%   | +6%   | +8%    | +10% |
| Spell Power         | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Travel CD           | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Weapon CD           | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Weapon Skill Power  | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |

Onyx TearCategoryAlchemyBloodboundNoTeleportableNoSalvageableNoMax Stack Size10DescriptionA black material forged by blood, gold and power. Used to restore the most powerful of the weapons.Produced at anAnvil.

# Stables

StablesResources8Iron Ingot12Stone Brick500Plant FibreUnlocked BySir Erwin the Gallant CavalierDescriptionAn animal pen that will automatically supply one horse with plant fibre. Feeding the horse nutrious plants will improve their attributes.TheStablesis aStructureused to feedHorsesand improve their stats. It is unlocked by defeatingSir Erwin the Gallant Cavalier.

After using theDominate MountVampire Power, it can also be used to unlock passive abilities for your vampire horse.

A horse may be "stored" in the stable by riding it into the stable and dismounting it. Its feed inventory will gradually be filled over time, without consuming anyPlant Fibrefrom your storage.

## Attribute Enhancement[]

Interacting with the stable while a horse is nearby allows the player to feed the horse with a flower stack. It will then begin consuming 1 flower every 6 seconds, increasing its associated stat by 0.01 per 2 flowers consumed. This is equivalent to 1 stat point gained per 20 minutes and per 200 flowers fed.

As each horse has their initial stats randomized within a range, the actual time and amount of flowers required to reach the stat cap will vary between horses. Vampire Horses have slightly higher stat caps. Refer to the table below.

| Stat           | Min Initial | Cap (Horse) | Cap (Vampire Horse) | Feed                                   | Max Feeding Required |
| -------------- | ----------- | ----------- | ------------------- | -------------------------------------- | -------------------- |
| Max Speed      | 7.5         | 9.5         | 10                  | SunflowerSnow FlowerFire Blossom       | 500                  |
| Acceleration   | 3.5         | 6           | 7                   | Hell's ClarionBlood RoseBleeding Heart | 700                  |
| Rotation Speed | 10          | 13          | 14                  | Sacred GrapesMourning LilyPlague Brier | 800                  |

## Vampire Horse Perks[]

While in the stables, click on the desired perk to feed elixirs to the Vampire Horse and unlock it. Refer to Table Below for elixir costs.

| Perk         | Unlock Requirement      | Effect                                                                                                                                                                           |
| ------------ | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Stability    | 4Elixir of the Beast    | 25% chance to avoid being dismounted when struck by an attack.                                                                                                                   |
| Athletics    | 4Elixir of the Prowler  | Vault off your mount faster with an agile leap.                                                                                                                                  |
| Eluding Leap | 4Elixir of the Crow     | Leave a decoy behind you to confuse nearby enemies when using shadow leap.                                                                                                       |
| Severance    | 4Elixir of the Werewolf | Next melee attack performed within3safter dismounting deals50%bonus damage.                                                                                                      |
| Thrust       | 4Elixir of the Twisted  | Unlocks a Thrust ability that allows you to knockback and incapacitate enemies in your path.Additionally you break any minor obstacles that you run into while thrust is active. |

---

# Shadowbolt

ShadowboltLaunch a projectile that deals 190% magic damage and inflictsLeech.Unlock RequirementDefault SpellMagic SchoolBloodClassBasic SpellTypeProjectile, Can CritCast Time1sCooldown8s

## Overview[]

Using this ability will heavily slow your character for the duration of the cast time, during this period ability can be cancelled. After cast time is complete without interruption, projectile will be released from position of your character in the direction of your cursor. After hitting enemy unit projectile will disappear. Hitting objects will also destroy projectile and deal damage to object hit, if possible.

In Hotfix #6, this spell's damage was increased from170%to185%.

In Update 1.1 this spell's damage was increased from185%to190%.

## Jewel Modifiers[]

| Jewel Modifiers [Tier 4]                                                                                                              |
| ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Hitting a target affected byLeechdeals30 - 50%bonus damage.                                                                           |
| Hitting a target affected byLeechheals self for1.9 - 3%of your maximum health.                                                        |
| Explodes on hit dealing19 - 30%damage and inflictingLeechon nearby enemies.                                                           |
| InflictsVampiric Cursedealing158 - 180%damage and leeching17 - 30%health after3sbut reduces damage done by the initial impact by140%. |
| Increase projectile range and speed by12 - 24%.                                                                                       |
| Increases cast rate by12 - 24%.                                                                                                       |
| Knock targets back1.6 - 3.2meters on hit.                                                                                             |
| Reduces cooldown by8 - 12%.                                                                                                           |

## Strategy[]

Shadowbolt is a spell with heavy damage, but also a long cast time that makes you vulnerable to enemy spells. The ability is great when combined with some kind of crowd control, like stun fromMerciless Charge, incapacitate from Slashers'Camouflageor aFreezeeffect. Best cast after an enemy has used their defensive spells.

## Video Showcase[]

## Change History[]

After theGloomrotupdate, Blood Magic Abilities applyLeechand spells can be socket byJewels(except for ultimates). Also, the magic damage was reduced from 200% to 180%.

It was further reduced to 170% in 1.0.

# Veil of Chaos

Veil of ChaosDash towards input direction and elude nearby enemies for 2.2s.Your next primary attack heals you for 5% of your maximum health, inflictsIgniteand allows you to recast the ability to dash once more. Your illusion explodes, dealing 50% magic damage to nearby enemies and inflictingIgnitewhen the effect ends.Unlock RequirementJade the Vampire HunterMagic SchoolChaosClassTravel SpellTypeVeil, Dash, Can CritCast Time0.3sCooldown8s

## Overview[]

The explosion knocks back regular enemies, but not enemy vampires.

After theGloomrotupdate, Chaos Magic Abilities applyIgnite. Also, your primary attack after the dash no longer deals 25% magic damage.

In Update 1.1 the Veil was changed to requiring landing a primary attack before the recast becomes available.

## Unlock Requirement[]

- Jade the Vampire Hunter


## Jewel Modifiers[]

| Jewel Modifiers [Tier 4]                                                                                                                                                |
| ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Next primary attack within3son a target affected byIgniteengulfs the target inAgonizing Flamesdealing2 - 6%damage and healing self for8 - 12%of your spell power5times. |
| Increases damage of next primary attack by12 - 24%.                                                                                                                     |
| Increases damage done when an illusion explodes by12 - 24%.                                                                                                             |
| Increases elude duration by10 - 20%.                                                                                                                                    |
| Inflicts a fading snare lasting0.8 - 1.6swhen an illusion explodes.                                                                                                     |
| Spawns a second illusion when recasting dealing40 - 80%of the original damage.                                                                                          |

# Void

VoidSummon an orb that explodes at the target location, dealing 90% magic damage, inflictingIgniteand pulls enemies towards the center.Unlock RequirementTier 2 Spell PointMagic SchoolChaosClassBasic SpellTypeTarget Area, Can CritCast Time0.3sCooldown9sCharges2

## Overview[]

After theGloomrotupdate, Chaos Magic Abilities applyIgnite. Also, the magic damage increased from 75% to 90%.

In Hotfix #9, this spell's damage radius was decreased from3.2to2.2. Time to impact was decreased from 1s to 0.8s. And knockback distance towards center was decreased from 2 to 1.

## Overview[]

After theGloomrotupdate, Chaos Magic Abilities applyIgnite. Also, Chaos Barrier do not increase movement speed natively anymore.  Was changed to fire only a single, charged projectile rather than one per attack blocked in 1.0.

# Merciless Charge

Merciless ChargeCharge forward and grab an enemy dealing 100% magic damage, and push them in front of you.Deals 250% magic area damage, inflictsIgniteand inflicts a Stun lasting 1s when reaching maximum range or when colliding with another enemy or object.Unlock RequirementTier 3 Spell PointMagic SchoolChaosClassUltimate SpellTypeTravel, Area, Cannot CritCast Time0.7sCooldown120s

## Overview[]

After theGloomrotupdate, Chaos Magic Abilities applyIgnite.  Also, magic area damage increased from 100% to 120%. Further increased to 125% in 1.0.

In Update 1.1 Merciless Charge received the following changes:

- Stun duration reduced to 1s from 1.5s.
- Stun now properly follows rules for diminishing returns.
- Dash damage reduced to 100% from 125%.
- Area damage increased to 250% from 125%.
- Removed the 0.15s invulnerability at the end of the Merciless Charge.


## Unlock Requirement[]

- Quincey the Bandit King
- Azariel the Sunbringer

Though not mentioned in the tooltip, Chaos Barrage inflicts a large knockback on impact.

Corrupted SkullLaunch a projectile that deals 80% magic damage, summons a skeleton and inflictsCondemn. The attack deals 40% bonus damage to enemies below 30% health.Unlock RequirementTier 1 Spell PointMagic SchoolUnholyClassBasic SpellTypeProjectile, Minion, Can CritCast Time0.7sCooldown8sCharges2

Skeleton Warrior/Skeleton Magehas health equal to200%of your Spell Power, and deals30%/50%of your Spell Power as magic damage. Theycannotcrit.

# Soulburn

SoulburnDrain the life from up to 3 nearby enemies dealing 50% magic damage, leeching 100% health, interrupting attacks and inflictingCondemn.Unlock RequirementTier 2 Spell PointMagic SchoolUnholyClassBasic SpellTypeArea, Can CritCast Time0.4sCooldown9s

## Overview[]

Was added inGloomrotupdate, and at the time unlocked by defeatingLord Styx the Night Champion.

InGloomrot Hotfix #7its silence duration nerfed from 2.5s to 1.5s.

In Update 1.0 its cast time was nerfed from 0.2 to 0.5s.

In Update 1.1 it was reworked entirely to no longer silence, instead dealing more damage and leeching more health. Although it still interrupts attacks, including barriers.

Skeleton Warrior/Skeleton Magehas health equal to200%of your Spell Power, and deals30%/50%of your Spell Power as magic damage. Theycannotcrit.

### Historical Mechanics[]

Soulburncould instantly cancel almost all non-counter playerspellsandweapon skills. If none were cancelled immediately, a unique "Spell Block" debuff will automatically cancel the player's next spell or weapon skill cast for ~0.7s. This includes primary attacks. Only if something is cancelled will the silence trigger.

Although it won't cancel counters, all its other effects still bypass them.

## Unlock Requirement[]

- Kriig the Undead General
- General Cassius the Betrayer
- Foulrot the Soultaker

| Jewel Modifiers [Tier 4]                                                                                             |

| Increases cast rate by12 - 24%.                                                                                      |
| Inflicts a fading snare on enemies hit lasting1.2 - 2.4s.                                                            |
| Shield self for24 - 40%of your spell power for each enemy hit.                                                       |
| Increases targets hit by1.                                                                                           |
| Increases life drain by12 - 24%                                                                                      |
| There is a60 - 100%chance to summon a skeleton warrior for each enemy hit.                                           |
| Increases damage by8 - 16%                                                                                           |

# Unholy Chains

Unholy ChainsLaunch a chain that shackles the target hit reducing movement speed by10%-30%based on distance to the target. Channel the spell for up to1.7s. Deals260%magic damage and inflictsCondemnwhen the effect ends.The bond breaks and inflicts a2sfading snare if the distance between yourself and the target exceeds14 meters.Unlock RequirementTier 2 Spell PointMagic SchoolUnholyClassBasic SpellTypeProjectile, Channelling, Can CritCast Time0.4sCooldown9s

## Overview[]

Added in Update 1.1. You're unable to perform any other actions besides movement duringUnholy Chains, or the effect ends.

However, because the spell is a projectile, it is possible to initiate channel spells during the projectile flight. Continuing these channels won't end the effect.

- General Cassius the Betrayer
- Foulrot the Soultaker

- Damage increased to170%from160%.

# Spectral Guardian

Spectral GuardianSummon a Spectral Guardian that shields allies in an area for 125% of your spell power and inflictsWeakenon nearby enemies. The guardian attacks enemies with a mighty swing dealing 150% magic damage. The shield is reapplied every 1.5s and the guardian lasts for 7s.Unlock RequirementTier 3 Spell PointMagic SchoolIllusionClassUltimate SpellTypeTarget Area, Minion, Cannot CritCast Time0.3sCooldown120s

## Overview[]

- Upon being summoned, the Spectral Guardian will knock back nearby enemies in the area.
- The Spectral Guadian swings roughly every 2 seconds, for a total of 3 swings per summon.


In Update 1.1 the Spectral Guardian's damage was increased from100%to150%.

- Terah the Geomancer
- Gorecrusher the Behemoth

# Wisp Dance

Wisp DanceSummon three wisps that circle around you, dealing 70% magic damage, leeching 30% health and inflictingWeakento enemies and grantingPhantasm.Recastto launch all three wisps as piercing projectiles dealing 125% magic damage, inflictingWeakenand grantingPhantasm.Unlock RequirementTier 3 Spell PointMagic SchoolIllusionClassUltimate SpellTypeProjectile, Lingering, Cannot CritCast Time0.2 sCooldown120 sRecast Time4s

## Overview[]

In theGloomrotexpansion this spell was changed from a basic to an ultimate spell. The wisps got increased in both size, speed and radius. Notably the damage was also changed from 25% to 60% magic damage in the first cast and from 50% to 100% magic damage in the recast.

In 1.0 the spell was buffed further, now leeching 30% health.

In Hotfix #9 this spell's damage was increased from100%to110%.

The initial cast cannot be countered.

In Update 1.1 this spell's damage was increased from60%to70%for the initial cast, and from110%to125%for the recast.

## Unlock Requirement[]

- Terah the Geomancer
- Gorecrusher the Behemoth


## Video Showcase[]

# Frost Bat

Frost BatLaunch a projectile that deals 120% magic damage. The projectile explodes upon impact, inflictingChillon nearby enemies. Hitting aChilledenemyFreezesit for 4s.Unlock RequirementTier 1 Spell PointMagic SchoolFrostClassBasic SpellTypeProjectile, Area, Can CritCast Time0.6sCooldown8sCharges2

## Overview[]

After the Gloomrot update, Frost Magic Abilities applyChill, which when applied on foes, slows their movement speed by 15% for 5s.

Additionally some abilities can inflictFreeze. Freezes your enemies solid, making them unable to move or act for 4s.

Deals 25% spell damage and inflictsChillif enemy is immune toFreeze.

Note:Vampires are frozen for half duration.

In Hotfix #6, this spell's damage was increased from100%to110%.

In Hotfix #9 this spell's damage was increased from110%to115%. The blast area's damage from the jewel modifier was increased by 20% as well.

In Update 1.1 this spell's damage was increased from115%to120%.

## Unlock Requirement[]

- Keely the Frost Archer
- Finn the Fisherman
- Sir Magnus the Overseer

# Cold Snap

Cold SnapBlock melee and projectile attacks for 1.5s. Blocking an attack triggers an ice nova that deals 50% magic damage and inflicts a 2sFreeze. Gain a shield absorbing up to 50% of your spell power for 4s when this effect triggers.Unlock RequirementTier 1 Spell PointMagic SchoolFrostClassBasic SpellTypeCounter, Area, Crowd Control, Cannot CritCast Time0.1sCooldown10s

## Overview[]

After the Gloomrot update, Frost Magic Abilities applyChill, which when applied on foes, slows their movement speed by 15% for 5s.

Additionally some abilities can inflictFreeze, which freezes your enemies solid, making them unable to move or act for 4s.

Deals 25% spell damage, inflictsChilland staggers the target for 1s if the target is immune toFreeze.

Vampires are frozen for half duration.

In Hotfix #6, this spell was nerfed in the following ways: Shield Duration reduced from 6s to 5s. Freeze Duration reduced from 3s to 2.5s Jewel boosting movement speed reduced from 10-25% to 10-15%

In Hotfix #9 this spell's shield value was decreased from100%to80%, and its freeze duration reduced from2.5sto2s.

In Update 1.1 this spell's shield value was decreased from80%to50%, and the duration lowered from5sto4s. The immaterial jewel modifier was also removed.

## Unlock Requirement[]

- Keely the Frost Archer
- Finn the Fisherman
- Sir Magnus the Overseer

# Discharge

DischargeBlock melee and projectile attacks for up to 1.5s. Blocking an attack pulls the target toward you and grants oneStorm Shield. Enemies triggering Discharge in close vicinity are stunned for 0.6s.Storm Shieldscircle around you, dealing 20% magic damage and inflictingStatic. Effect stacks up to 3 times.Unlock RequirementTier 1 Spell PointMagic SchoolStormClassBasic SpellTypeCounter, Crowd Control, Cannot CritCast Time0.1sCooldown10s

## Overview[]

Unlike other counters, Discharge can block an indefinite amount of attacks. Storm Shields last for 5s.

### Discharge's History[]

Dischargewas originally added in theGloomrotupdate. It read as follows prior to the rework in the 1.0 Update:

Block melee and projectile attacks for up to 1.5s. Turn immaterial and travel to cursor location when an attack is blocked.Passing through an enemy deals 50% magic damage, inflictsStaticand launches the target into the air for 3s. Cooldown: 9s.

In its current iteration, it was nerfed in Hotfix #6:

- Stun duration reduced to 0.6s from 0.8s.
- Jewel that allows you to recast, damage reduced from 25 - 50% to 15 - 30% and knockback effect power reduced by ~25%.
- Jewel increasing stun duration reduced from 0.2 - 0.4s to 0.1 - 0.3s.
- Jewel granting immaterial, duration reduced from 0.8 - 1.6s to 0.8 - 1.2s


### Post Invaders of Oakveil[]

Following the 1.1 update - Invaders of Oakveil -  Discharge was changed in the following ways

- The immaterial jewel was removed.
- Targets triggering the counter are no longer subjected to the stun or knockback effect if they're immaterial when the trigger happens. Static is still inflicted.
- The recast jewel now inflicts a fading snare rather than knockback (no longer interrupting casts).


## Unlock Requirement[]

- Sir Erwin the Gallant Cavalier
- Grethel the Glassblower
- Mairwyn the Elementalist

# Blood Spray

Blood SprayIncreases Physical Critical Chance by8%. Critical Strikes leech5%health and there is a25%chance to spawn aBlood Orbwhen killing a target affected byLeech.Unlock Requirement400Stygian ShardsMagic SchoolBloodClassPassive

## Overview[]

Passive abilities can be unlocked at theAltar of Stygian Awakeningin exchange forStygian ShardsandGreater Stygian Shards.

Players may unlock all passives, but only have up to 5Passive Slotsavailable. Similar to theResearch Desk, players may collectively unlock and share passives within their clan.

# Sanguine Mastery

Sanguine MasteryDeal8%increased physical damage to enemies affected byLeechand boost the effect of your current blood type by8%.Unlock Requirement400Stygian ShardsMagic SchoolBloodClassPassive

## Overview[]

This passive works additively with other blood efficiency bonuses. Stats gained this way raises yourstat cap.

The Angel deals damage and applies Condemn in an area when summoned.

# Blood Coating

Blood CoatingCategoryConsumableBloodboundNoTeleportableYesSalvageableNoMax Stack Size10DescriptionImbue your equipped weapon with the essence of blood. Your next primary attack inflictsLeechandVampiric Curse, dealing40%magic damage after2sand spawning aBlood Orb.The on hit effect recharges every12sand the imbuement lasts for60 minutes.Effect persists through death.

Blood Coatingis a craftedconsumableitem.

It does not stack with otherimbuements. The most recently consumed one will override the other.

# Holy Resistance Flask

Holy Resistance FlaskCategoryConsumableBloodboundNoTeleportableYesSalvageableNoMax Stack Size10DescriptionA potion that increasesholyresistance rating by75for60 minutes.Effect persists through death.

Holy Resistance Flaskis a craftedconsumableitem. It can be purchased from theCity Herb & Potion VendororTreasure Hunter Trade Postfor60Goldsun Coins.

Holy Resistance protects the user fromHoly Radiationfound in Dunley Monastery (Raziel the Shepherd), Brighthaven Cathedral (Azariel the Sunbringer) and Fortress of Light (Solarus the Immaculate).

Holy Resistance FlaskDoes not stack withHoly Resistance Potion. The most recently consumed one will override the other.

# Irradiant Gruel

Irradiant GruelCategoryConsumableBloodboundNoTeleportableYesSalvageableNoMax Stack Size20DescriptionA brew with blood-mutating effects. Not recommended to drink.

Irradiant Gruelis a craftedconsumableitem. It increases the blood quality of aprisonerby+1% ~ +2%, but has a35% chanceto turn the prisoner into a raging mutant.

The Mutant created will always be the mutantAbominationand cannot bedominated. Irradiant gruel is not a method of obtaining 100% mutant blood. If a prisoner is transformed into anabomination, it must be killed.

## Crafting[]

| Item            | Materials                               | Structure     | Unlocked by         |
| --------------- | --------------------------------------- | ------------- | ------------------- |
| Irradiant Gruel | 20 (15)Plague Brier20 (15)Mutant Grease | Alchemy Table | Angram the Purifier |

## Trivia[]

- Drinking theIrradiant Gruelputs you in combat and deals damage over time for a few seconds.
- It is possible to obtain Irradiant Gruel as a rare random loot in the Gloomrot, but the player will be unable to feed it to prisoners until they have defeatedAngram the Purifier.

# Major Explosive Box

Major Explosive BoxCategoryConsumableBloodboundNoTeleportableNoSalvageableNoMax Stack Size5DescriptionA box full of explosives, handle with care. Can be used to destroy Massive Resource Veins, Walls and Doors. More powerful against castle walls.The Major Explosive Box is a recipe obtained fromAngram the Purifier. This is the second raiding method players get access to. It is used to destroy stone structures by moving it to the hotbar and placing it down.

Once the fuse is lit by any weapon attack or spell, includingenemyattacks, it will explode after 3 seconds. It does 40% of a structure's max health in damage, meaning it requires 3 boxes to fully destroy a structure.Note that explosives can only damage stone structuresafterthey have beenbreachedby aSiege Golem.

It can also be used for mining large resource deposits located throughout the map that can't be mined by traditional means, likemaces.The MEB also has offensive and defensive uses in combat against players and monsters alike, however it is difficult to pull off.

# Dusk Caller

Dusk CallerCategoryConsumableBloodboundNoTeleportableYesSalvageableNoMax Stack Size5DescriptionSummon a swarm of bats to transport a subdued human back to the nearest unoccupied prison cell within your realm.Produced at anAlchemy Lab.

Dusk Calleris a craftedconsumableitem. It allows you to summon a swarm of bats to transport a subdued human back to the nearest unoccupiedPrison Cellwithin your realm. Can only be used whileDominateis active.

If you're in a clan, it will transport the human to nearest unoccupied prison cell within all your castles. If you'd like to ensure the target is transported to a specific prison cell, make sure that cell is the only unoccupied one at the time.

# Garlic Resistance Potion

Garlic Resistance PotionCategoryConsumableBloodboundNoTeleportableYesSalvageableNoMax Stack Size10DescriptionA potion that increasesgarlicresistance rating by80for60 minutes.Effect persists through death.

Garlic Resistance Potionis a craftedconsumableitem. It can be purchased from theCity Herb & Potion VendororTreasure Hunter Trade Postfor20Goldsun Coins. The blueprint can also be acquired from theShady Book Dealerfor64Silver Coins.

Garlic Resistance causesGarlic Exposurestacks from Cotton Farms in theDunley Farmlandsto accumulate at a slower rate and drop off faster.
