# Minor Explosive Box

Minor Explosive BoxCategoryConsumableBloodboundNoTeleportableNoSalvageableNoMax Stack Size5DescriptionA box full of explosives, handle with care. Can be used to destroy Massive Resource Veins, Walls and Doors.The Minor Explosive Box is a recipe obtained fromClive the Firestarter. This is the first raiding method players get access to. It is used to destroy wooden structures by moving it to the hotbar and placing it down. It is notably used to enterQuincey the Bandit King's stronghold.

Once the fuse is lit by any weapon attack or spell, includingenemyattacks, it will explode after 3 seconds. It does 20% of a structure's max health in damage, meaning it requires 5 boxes to fully destroy a structure.

It can also be used for mining large resource deposits located throughout the map that can't be mined by traditional means, likemaces.The Minor Explosive Box also has offensive and defensive uses in combat against players and monsters alike, however it is difficult to pull off.

# Blood Rose Brew

Blood Rose BrewCategoryConsumableBloodboundNoTeleportableYesSalvageableNoMax Stack Size10DescriptionA brew that recovers40%of your maximum health over10s. The healing effect is limited when in combat and breaks upon taking damage.

Blood Rose Brewis a craftedconsumableitem. It can be purchased from theShady Herb & Potion Dealerfor18Copper Coins.

## Crafting[]

| Item            | Materials                         | Structure            | Unlocked By   |
| --------------- | --------------------------------- | -------------------- | ------------- |
| Blood Rose Brew | 32 (24)Blood Rose1Empty Waterskin | By HandAlchemy Table | Research Desk |

## Healing Mechanics[]

The healing effects fromVermin Salve,Blood Rose BrewandBlood Rose Potionstack on top of each other. Cast Time: ~1.5 s.However, while in combat you're only able to recover up to 25% Max HP at a time. For example, if you're at 50% health, you can only heal up to 75% max health until you leave combat.Blood Orbsbypass this limitation.

---

# Treasury Flooring

Treasury FlooringAffluentPrizedProsperousNocturnal Opulence *DLCRoomTreasuryResources4Stone Brick2Gem DustUnlocked ByNicholaus the Fallen

Treasury Flooringis a type ofCastle Flooravailable in V Rising. Upon changingall the flooringof a castle room, it activates theTreasuryRoom bonus to allow access tostorage structureswithin the room from anywhere in the castle when crafting orBuilding.

The blueprint is unlocked by defeatingNicholaus the Fallen.

It is available in 4 different patterns, which have no differences besides aesthetics. The Nocturnal Opulence Treasury Tiles are exclusive to theEternal Dominance PackDLC.

# Leatherworking Station

Leatherworking StationRoomTailorResources12Plank12LeatherUnlocked ByLidia the Chaos ArcherDescriptionA workstation used for shaping leather into bags and various items.Dimensions1x1

Leatherworking Stationis a workstation used for shaping leather into bags and various horse saddles.

## Perks[]

- In Confined Castle Room: +25% speed.
- Has Matching Floor(Tailor's Flooring): -25% material cost.

# Artisan Table

Artisan TableRoomJeweller's ChamberResources1Greater Blood Essence4Scourgestone16Iron IngotUnlocked ByLeandra the Shadow PriestessDescriptionA workstation used for crafting of magical objects.Dimensions2x1

Artisan Tableis a workstation used for crafting of magical objects (Jewelry). It is preceded by theSimple Workbench.

## Perks[]

- In Confined Castle Room: +25% speed.
- Has Matching Floor(Jeweller's Chamber Floor): -25% material cost.


## Recipes[]

Jewelry, also classified asMagic Sourcesin the game, amplifies the power of vampirespells.Higher tiers can also offer other stat bonuses, such as Physical Power. For spell modifiers seeJewels.

# Gem Cutting Table

Gem Cutting TableRoomJeweller's ChamberResources12Iron Ingot60Gem Dust24Stone BrickUnlocked ByTerah the GeomancerDescriptionA workstation used for combining lower quality gems into higher quality gems.Dimensions1x1

Gem Cutting Tableis a workstation used for combining lower quality gems into higher quality gems. By default the station only allows for the crafting of Regular Gems. Flawless gemcutting is unlocked onceMorian the Stormwing Matriarchis defeated.

## Perks[]

- In Confined Castle Room: +25% speed.
- Has Matching Floor(Jeweller's Chamber Floor): -25% material cost.

# Jewelcrafting Table

Jewelcrafting TableRoomJeweller's ChamberResources4Greater Blood Essence8Scourgestone64Gem DustUnlocked ByRaziel the ShepherdDescriptionA workstation used for crafting jewels.Dimensions1x1

TheJewelcrafting Tableallows for the crafting of powerfulJewelsthat can modify all non-ultimate spells in the game. Spell jewels can only be socketed into unlocked spells, but will remain socketed after spell point resets at theAltar of Recollection.

Jewels come in 4 tiers;Tier 1,Tier 2,Tier 3, &Tier 4.Each tier corresponds to the number of modifiers it has.For example,Tier 2 Jewels will have 2 modifiers.

Modifiers themselves also come in 5 tiers, though some unique modifiers only have 1 tier. It is speculated that higher tier Jewels possess a greater chance of rolling higher tier modifiers.

They're always found in Golden Chests &Caravancontainers, and commonly drop fromV Blood Carriers, duringRift Incursionsand rarely even regularenemies. No matter how they're acquired, the jewel's name, its modifiers, and their respective tiers are always randomized. For a list of all the modifiers, seeJewels.

## Perks[]

- In Confined Castle Room: +25% speed.
- Has Matching Floor(Jeweller's Chamber Floor): -25% material cost.

# Ancestral Forge

Ancestral ForgeRoomForgeResources1Primal Blood Essence8Radium Alloy16Iron IngotUnlocked ByOctavian the Militia CaptainDescriptionA workstation used for restoring ancient shattered weapons.Dimensions1x1

## Overview[]

Merciless & SanguineWeaponscan be upgraded at the Ancestral Forge into Rare & EpicAncestral Weaponsrespectively. Crafting ancestral weapons requires anancestral weapon shard, the attributes of which are alwaysrandomly generated. Rare ancestrals can be further upgraded fromGear Level20, to 24, to 27.

All ancestral weapons are randomly infused with aSpell Schooldebuff as well, causing SecondWeapon Skill(Q) hits to inflictLeech/Ignite/Condemn/Weaken/Chill/Static.

## Perks[]

- In Confined Castle Room: +25% speed.
- Has Matching Floor(Forge Floor): -25% material cost.


## Possible Attribute Rolls[]

RareandEpicAncestral weapons have2and3randomattributes respectively. Each attribute has a minimum base value, which is then randomly multiplied by 1, 2, 3, 4, or 5. There are 14 different attributes in total. Refer to the table below:

| Attribute                  | 1     | 2     | 3     | 4      | 5    |
| -------------------------- | ----- | ----- | ----- | ------ | ---- |
| Bonus Maximum Health       | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Bonus Movement Speed       | +1.6% | +3.2% | +4.8% | +6.4%  | +8%  |
| Veil Cooldown Rate         | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Bonus Physical Power       | +2%   | +4%   | +6%   | +8%    | +10% |
| Attack Speed               | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Weapon Skill Cooldown Rate | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Weapon Skill Power         | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Physical Critical Chance   | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Physical Critical Power    | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Bonus Spell Power          | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Spell Cooldown Rate        | +2.8% | +5.6% | +8.4% | +11.2% | +14% |
| Spell Critical Chance      | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Spell Critical Power       | +3.2% | +6.4% | +9.6% | +12.8% | +16% |
| Spell Leech                | +2%   | +4%   | +6%   | +8%    | +10% |

## Recipes[]

Rare Ancestral Weapon Shardscan be purchased at the southernVampire Merchantfor750Stygian Shardeach, dropped by level 53+V Bloodsor fromTier 1 Rift Incursions.

Epic Ancestral Weapon Shardscan be purchased at the northernVampire Merchantfor1500Greater Stygian Shardeach, dropped by level 77+V Bloodsor fromTier 2 Rift Incursions.

Legendary Ancestral Weapon Shardshave a 15% chance of replacing an Epic Weapon Shard whenever it's acquired by any means.

# Fusion Forge

Fusion ForgeRoomForgeResources1Primal Blood Essence12Ember Glass16Dark Silver IngotUnlocked ByDantos the ForgebinderDescriptionA workstation used for fusing weapons or jewels.Dimensions1x1

## Overview[]

TheFusion Forgeprovides two slots where you can placeanytwoAncestral Weapons(shattered or reforged) or twoJewelsfor the same spell. The highest level attributes will be combined into a single list, from which you must select which to keep and which to discard in order to fit within the maximum number of attributes allowed on the item.

Fusing attributes onto the primary item costs12 (9)Ember Glass, and destroys the secondary item in the process.

## Perks[]

- In Confined Castle Room: +25% speed.
- Has Matching Floor(Forge Floor): -25% material cost.


---

# The Devourer

The DevourerRoomGeneralResources12Plank6Copper IngotUnlocked ByLidia the Chaos ArcherDescriptionThe Devourer can tear apart equipment, items and components, turning them into raw materials.Dimensions1x1

The Devourercan tear apart equipment, items and components, turning them into raw materials. 
Refined materials can be salvaged into a quarter of their base crafting cost.

Weapons & armours' number of salvaged materials scales with higher current durability.

# Castle Throne

Castle ThroneCastle ThroneRoyal Throne *DLCPlague Chemist's Throne *DLCAncient Symphony Throne *DLCResources24Stone Brick12Copper Ingot4Grave Dust1Greater Blood EssenceUnlocked ByArmy of Darkness(Quest)

| “ | Sit down in the Throne and command your servants. Send them to hunt for treasure, knowledge and blood. | ” |
| - | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | - |

The Castle Throne is aDominationstructure unlocked by completing the QuestArmy of Darkness. It is required to complete the QuestQuest: Throne of Command(Crypt Flooring), and used to sendServantsonHunts.

Once you have placed down your throne, you can send yourServantson Hunts in different locations that you have discovered. When selecting the destination, you can choose the duration of the hunt (varies from 2 - 16 hours ofREAL TIME) which will affect both the success rate and the quantity of resources brought back.

Servant Coffinsmust be within approx. 14 tiles of the Castle Throne in order to be assigned to hunts.

If a hunt fails, your servant will be killed and will need to be revived before being sent out again.

## Servant Hunts[]

## Servant Blood Type & Faction Perks[]

Servants have 2 perks that each will provide a benefit when going on hunts in which the perks are active.

The first perk is based onBlood Type, and will reduce the difficulty of a Hunt in a given location by 100.The second perk is determined by their faction, ie.locationof origin, increasing loot gained from successful hunts in that region by 20%.

Blood Type Perks do not stack, so sending a diverse group of servants on hunts is advised.

| Blood Type         | Servant Perk       | Description                                                                                                                                                                |
| ------------------ | ------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Worker             | Humble Appearance  | Reduces Difficulty by100when infiltrating settlements.                                                                                                                     |
| Scholar            | Sacred Resistance  | Reduces Difficulty by100when hunting in areas protected by the elements.                                                                                                   |
| Brute              | Tenacious Strength | Reduces Difficulty by100when hunting in harsh environments.                                                                                                                |
| Rogue              | Tracking Expertise | Reduces Difficulty by100when hunting in areas inhabited by creatures and demons.                                                                                           |
| Warrior / Draculin | Military Tactics   | Reduces Difficulty by100when hunting in fortified areas.                                                                                                                   |
| Corrupted          | Enemy Dependent    | Corrupted human enemies have mixed blood. Their original blood type will determine their first perk. (eg. a Corrupted Peon with Worker Blood will have Humble Appearance.) |

| Location / Faction | Servant Perk            | Description                                                                            |
| ------------------ | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Farbane Woods      | Farbane Hunter          | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Farbane Woods by20%.     |
| Dunley Farmlands   | Dunley Farmlands Hunter | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Dunley Farmlands by20%.  |
| Cursed Forest      | Cursed Forest Hunter    | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Cursed Forest by20%.     |
| Silverlight Hills  | Silverlight Hunter      | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Silverlight Hills by20%. |
| Gloomrot           | Gloomrot Hunter         | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Gloomrot by20%.          |
| Ruins of Mortium   | Ruins of Mortium Hunter | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Ruins of Mortium by20%.  |
| Oakveil Woodlands  | Oakveil Hunter          | Increases the amount of loot secured from successful hunts in Oakveil Woodlands by20%. |

## Tips & Trivia[]

- Servants and the hunts they're sent on are tied to the territory'sCastle Heart. This means you can send servants from different territories to hunt at the same location simultaneously.
- Cursed Forest Hunter Perk is currently exclusive to Werewolf Workers fromGracefall Village, including those few wandering the roads ofDunley Farmlands.As a Servant they will no longer transform, only whenimprisoned.
- Corrupted humanenemieswith theOakveil Hunter Perk have mixed blood. Their original blood type will determine their first perk.
- Theonlydraculin units that may be converted into Servants are Vampire Cultists, Night Maidens, Dark Temptresses and Exsanguinators.


## Throne Variations[]

There are multiple variations of the Castle Throne available. They have no differences in function besides aesthetics:

- Royal Throne, which is available through theDracula's Relics PackDLC.
- Plague Chemist's Throne, which is available through theSinister Evolution PackDLC.
- Ancient Symphony Throne, which is available through theLegacy of Castlevania Premium PackDLC.
- Nocturnal Opulence Throne, which is available through theEternal Dominance PackDLC.


---
